<script>
	const mobileNavOpen = document.querySelector( 'header#masthead #mobileMenuOpen' );
	const mobileNavClose = document.querySelector( 'header#masthead #mobileMenuClose' );
	const mobilePrimaryMenu = document.querySelector( 'header#masthead nav#site-navigation ul#menu-primary-menu' );

	document.querySelectorAll('header#masthead ul#menu-primary-menu li span.dropdown-menu-toggle').forEach(item => {
		item.addEventListener( 'click', function( event ){
			event.preventDefault();
			let thisParentBgColor = getComputedStyle(this.parentNode).backgroundColor;
			if( thisParentBgColor == '#FC392D' ){
				this.parentNode.parentNode.querySelector( 'ul.sub-menu').style.display = 'none';
				this.parentNode.style.backgroundColor = 'rgb(48, 63, 71)';
			} else {
				document.querySelectorAll('header#masthead ul#menu-primary-menu li ul.sub-menu').forEach(liUlItem => {
					liUlItem.style.display = 'none';
				});
				document.querySelectorAll('header#masthead ul#menu-primary-menu>li.menu-item-has-children>a').forEach(liItem => {
					liItem.style.backgroundColor = 'rgb(48, 63, 71)';
				});
				this.parentNode.style.backgroundColor = '#FC392D';
				this.parentNode.parentNode.querySelector( 'ul.sub-menu').style.display = 'block';
			}
		});
	});
	mobileNavOpen.addEventListener( 'click', function( event ) {

        let element = document.getElementById("site-navigation");
        element.classList.add("toggled");

        // Activate bg-overlay
        document.querySelector(".bg-overlay").classList.add("active-overlay");



		let elemClass = mobileNavOpen.getAttribute( 'class' );
		mobileNavOpen.setAttribute( 'class', 'd-none' );
		mobileNavClose.setAttribute( 'class', 'd-block' );
		mobilePrimaryMenu.style.display = 'block';
	})
	mobileNavClose.addEventListener( 'click', function( event ) {

        let element = document.getElementById("site-navigation");
        element.classList.remove("toggled");

        // Disable bg-overlay
        document.querySelector(".bg-overlay").classList.remove("active-overlay");

		let elemClass = mobileNavClose.getAttribute( 'class' );
		mobileNavClose.setAttribute( 'class', 'd-none' );
		mobileNavOpen.setAttribute( 'class', 'd-block' );
		mobilePrimaryMenu.style.display = 'none';
	})
</script>
